 477029         // ========== Helper Functions ==========
 477080         
 477090         /**
 477103          * Get supported language code from browser language
 477165          */
 477178         function getSupportedLanguage(lang) {
 477225             // First try exact match
 477263             if (languageMap[lang]) {
 477301                 return languageMap[lang];
 477344             }
 477359             // Then try to match only the main language code
 477421             const mainLang = lang.split('-')[0];
 477471             if (languageMap[mainLang]) {
 477513                 return languageMap[mainLang];
 477560             }
 477575             // If no match, return English
 477619             return 'en-US';
 477648         }
 477661         /**
 477674          * Change the page language
 477711          */
 477724         function changeLanguage() {
 477761             const lang = document.getElementById('language').value;
 477830             
 477844             // Check if language is valid
 477887             if (!translations[lang]) {
 477927                 console.warn(`Unsupported language: ${lang}, defaulting to English`);
 478014                 document.getElementById('language').value = 'en-US';
 478084                 return changeLanguage();
 478126             }
 478141             
 478155             // Set page title
 478186             document.title = translations[lang].title;
 478242             
 478256             // Update text content
 478292             document.querySelectorAll('[data-lang]').forEach(element => {
 478367                 const key = element.getAttribute('data-lang');
 478431                 element.textContent = translations[lang][key];
 478495             });
 478512             
 478526             // Update input values
 478562             document.querySelectorAll('[data-lang-value]').forEach(element => {
 478643                 const key = element.getAttribute('data-lang-value');
 478713                 element.value = translations[lang][key];
 478771             });
 478788             
 478802             // Update AP list text based on 5G support
 478858             const apList = document.getElementById('ap_list');
 478922             if (apList.firstChild) {
 478960                 const selectText = support5G ? translations[lang].select_wifi_5g : translations[lang].select_wifi;
 479076                 apList.firstChild.textContent = selectText;
 479137             }
 479152             
 479166             // Save language preference
 479207             localStorage.setItem('preferred_language', lang);
 479270         }
 479283         // ========== Wi-Fi List Management ==========
 479339         
 479349         /**
 479362          * Render saved Wi-Fi list
 479398          */
 479411         function renderSavedList(data) {
 479453             const savedListContainer = document.getElementById('saved_list_container');
 479542             const savedList = document.getElementById('saved_list');
 479612             savedList.innerHTML = '';
 479651             
 479665             data.forEach((ssid, index) => {
 479710                 const li = document.createElement('li');
 479768                 let html = `<span>${ssid}</span>`;
 479820                 
 479838                 // Only add priority and delete buttons after the first item
 479916                 if (index > 0) {
 479950                     html += ` <span>
 479988                         <button type="button" onclick="setDefaultItem(this, ${index})">
 480081 </button>
 480092                         <button type="button" onclick="deleteItem(this, ${index})">
 480178 </button>
 480189                     </span>`;
 480220                 } else {
 480246                     html += ` <span><button type="button" onclick="deleteItem(this, ${index})">
 480344 </button></span>`;
 480364                 }
 480383                 
 480401                 li.innerHTML = html;
 480439                 savedList.appendChild(li);
 480483             });
 480500             
 480514             // Show/hide container based on whether there are saved networks
 480592             savedListContainer.style.display = data.length > 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
 480676         }
 480689         /**
 480702          * Delete saved Wi-Fi network
 480741          */
 480754         function deleteItem(item, index) {
 480798             item.disabled = true;
 480833             fetch('/saved/delete?index=' + index)
 480884                 .then(response => response.json())
 480936                 .then(data => {
 480969                     loadSavedList();
 481007                 });
 481028         }
 481041         /**
 481054          * Set default Wi-Fi network (move to top)
 481106          */
 481119         function setDefaultItem(item, index) {
 481167             item.disabled = true;
 481202             fetch('/saved/set_default?index=' + index)
 481258                 .then(response => response.json())
 481310                 .then(data => {
 481343                     loadSavedList();
 481381                 });
 481402         }
 481415         /**
 481428          * Load saved Wi-Fi list from server
 481474          */
 481487         function loadSavedList() {
 481523             fetch('/saved/list')
 481557                 .then(response => response.json())
 481609                 .then(data => {
 481642                     renderSavedList(data);
 481686                 });
 481707         }
 481720         /**
 481733          * Load available Wi-Fi networks
 481775          */
 481788         function loadAPList() {
 481821             if (button.disabled) {
 481857                 return;
 481882             }
 481899             const lang = document.getElementById('language').value;
 481968             const apList = document.getElementById('ap_list');
 482034             // Check if AP list already has content
 482087             const hasExistingAPs = apList.querySelector('a') !== null;
 482161             // Only show scanning text if there's no existing AP list
 482232             if (!hasExistingAPs) {
 482268                 apList.innerHTML = '<p class="scanning">' + translations[lang].scanning + '</p>';
 482367             }
 482384             fetch('/scan')
 482412                 .then(response => response.json())
 482464                 .then(data => {
 482497                     // Update global 5G support status
 482553                     support5G = data.support_5g;
 482603                     
 482625                     // Use select_wifi_5g if 5G is supported, otherwise use select_wifi
 482714                     const selectText = support5G ? translations[lang].select_wifi_5g : translations[lang].select_wifi;
 482834                     apList.innerHTML = '<p>' + selectText + '</p>';
 482903                     
 482925                     // Iterate through available APs
 482979                     data.aps.forEach(ap => {
 483025                         const link = document.createElement('a');
 483092                         link.href = '#';
 483134                         link.textContent = ap.ssid + ' (' + ap.rssi + ' dBm)';
 483214                         
 483240                         // Add lock icon for secured networks
 483303                         if (ap.authmode === 0) {
 483353                             link.textContent += ' 
 483411                         } else {
 483445                             link.textContent += ' 
 483503                         }
 483530                         
 483556                         link.addEventListener('click', () => {
 483620                             ssid.value = ap.ssid;
 483671                         });
 483700                         
 483726                         apList.appendChild(link);
 483777                     });
 483802                     
 483824                     // Refresh AP list every 5 seconds
 483880                     setTimeout(loadAPList, 5000);
 483931                 })
 483951                 .catch(error => {
 483986                     console.error('Error:', error);
 484039                     // On error, try again after 5 seconds
 484099                     setTimeout(loadAPList, 5000);
 484150                 });
 484171         }
 484184         // ========== Form Submission ==========
 484234         
 484244         /**
 484257          * Submit Wi-Fi connection form
 484298          */
 484311         async function submitForm(event) {
 484355             event.preventDefault();
 484392             button.disabled = true;
 484429             error.textContent = '';
 484468             // Show loading animation
 484507             const loadingOverlay = document.getElementById('loadingOverlay');
 484586             loadingOverlay.classList.add('show');
 484639             const payload = {
 484670                 ssid: ssid.value,
 484705                 password: document.getElementById('password').value
 484774             };
 484792             try {
 484811                 const response = await fetch('/submit', {
 484870                     method: 'POST',
 484907                     headers: {
 484939                         'Content-Type': 'application/json'
 484999                     },
 485023                     body: JSON.stringify(payload)
 485074                 });
 485097                 const data = await response.json();
 485150                 if (!data.success) {
 485188                     throw new Error(data.error || 'Connection failed');
 485261                 }
 485282                 // Connection successful, redirect to done page
 485347                 button.disabled = false;
 485389                 window.location.href = '/done.html';
 485443             } catch (err) {
 485472                 // Hide loading animation on error
 485524                 loadingOverlay.classList.remove('show');
 485582                 error.textContent = err.message;
 485632                 button.disabled = false;
 485674             }
 485689         }
 485702         /**
 485715          * Submit advanced configuration form
 485762          */
 485775         async function submitAdvancedForm(event) {
 485827             event.preventDefault();
 485864             const advancedButton = document.getElementById('advanced_button');
 485944             const advancedError = document.getElementById('advanced_error');
 486022             advancedButton.disabled = true;
 486067             advancedError.textContent = '';
 486114             const config = {
 486144                 ota_url: document.getElementById('ota_url').value,
 486212                 max_tx_power: parseInt(document.getElementById('max_tx_power').value),
 486300                 remember_bssid: document.getElementById('remember_bssid').checked,
 486384                 sleep_mode: document.getElementById('sleep_mode').checked
 486459             };
 486477             try {
 486496                 const response = await fetch('/advanced/submit', {
 486564                     method: 'POST',
 486601                     headers: {
 486633                         'Content-Type': 'application/json'
 486693                     },
 486717                     body: JSON.stringify(config)
 486767                 });
 486790                 const data = await response.json();
 486843                 if (!data.success) {
 486881                     throw new Error(data.error || 'Save failed');
 486948                 }
 486969                 advancedButton.disabled = false;
 487019                 showToast('Configuration saved');
 487070             } catch (err) {
 487099                 advancedError.textContent = err.message;
 487157                 advancedButton.disabled = false;
 487207             }
 487222         }
 487235         // ========== UI Functions ==========
 487282         
 487292         /**
 487305          * Switch between tabs
 487337          */
 487350         function switchTab(tabName) {
 487389             // Hide all tab contents
 487427             document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => {
 487503                 content.classList.remove('active');
 487556             });
 487573             
 487587             // Remove active class from all tabs
 487637             document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(tab => {
 487701                 tab.classList.remove('active');
 487750             });
 487767             
 487781             // Show selected tab content
 487823             document.getElementById(tabName + '-tab').classList.add('active');
 487903             
 487917             // Activate selected tab
 487955             document.querySelector(`.tab[onclick="switchTab('${tabName}')"]`).classList.add('active');
 488059         }
 488072         /**
 488085          * Show toast notification
 488121          */
 488134         function showToast(message) {
 488173             const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
 488234             toast.textContent = message;
 488276             toast.classList.add('show');
 488318             setTimeout(() => {
 488350                 toast.classList.remove('show');
 488399             }, 3000);
 488422         }
 488435         /**
 488448          * Load advanced configuration from server
 488500          */
 488513         async function loadAdvancedConfig() {
 488560             try {
 488579                 const response = await fetch('/advanced/config');
 488646                 const data = await response.json();
 488699                 
 488717                 if (data.ota_url) {
 488754                     document.getElementById('ota_url').value = data.ota_url;
 488832                 }
 488851                 if (data.max_tx_power) {
 488893                     document.getElementById('max_tx_power').value = data.max_tx_power;
 488981                 }
 489000                 if (data.remember_bssid !== undefined) {
 489058                     document.getElementById('remember_bssid').checked = data.remember_bssid;
 489152                 }
 489171                 if (data.sleep_mode !== undefined) {
 489225                     document.getElementById('sleep_mode').checked = data.sleep_mode;
 489311                 }
 489330             } catch (error) {
 489361                 console.error('Error loading advanced config:', error);
 489434             }
 489449         }
 489462         /**
 489475          * Clear OTA URL input field
 489513          */
 489526         function clearOtaUrl() {
 489560             document.getElementById('ota_url').value = '';
 489620         }
 489633         // ========== Initialization ==========
 489682         
 489692         /**
 489705          * Initialize page on DOM load
 489745          */
 489758         document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
 489821             // Get language setting from URL parameters
 489878             const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
 489954             const langParam = urlParams.get('lang');
 490008             
 490022             // Get browser language
 490059             const browserLang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
 490138             
 490152             // Priority: URL parameter > local storage > browser language setting
 490235             const savedLang = langParam || 
 490280                              localStorage.getItem('preferred_language') || 
 490357                              getSupportedLanguage(browserLang);
 490422             
 490436             document.getElementById('language').value = savedLang;
 490504             changeLanguage();
 490535             loadSavedList();
 490565             loadAPList();
 490592             loadAdvancedConfig();
 490627         });
 490642         /**
 490655          * Handle browser back button
 490694          */
 490707         window.addEventListener('pageshow', (event) => {
 490765             if (event.persisted) {
 490801                 loadSavedList();
 490835             }
 490850         });
 490865         /**
 490878          * Enable SSID input (fix iOS bug)
 490922          */
 490935         ssid.addEventListener('touchstart', () => {
